Both sources confirm that the scientific name is currently accepted and valid.

Please note that the actual date recorded on the label ("date=21-35") is somewhat ambiguous and does not conform to standard date representations. It was interpreted as the 21st to the 35th of May, 1935, but since there are only 31 days in May, the exact day within the month cannot be precisely determined beyond the 21st.

Following the instruction to check for the accepted scientific name and details, here is what was found after a search via the provided authority websites:

After searching for "Lavandula pubescens" in the Global Biodiversity Information Facility (GBIF), I found that the accepted scientific name for this species remains Lavandula pubescens Decaisne. It is classified in the family Lamiaceae, within the phylum (division) Tracheophyta (which is the scientific term for vascular plants), and the genus Lavandula. There is no infraspecific epithet as this taxon is not subdivided further within this species.
